URN:CornellLabOfOrnithology:EBIRD:OBS265887086	2018-12-25 13:24:08	26120	species	Canyon Wren	Catherpes mexicanus			3				United States	US	Nevada	US-NV	White Pine	US-NV-033		9			Unnamed Canyon in Butte Mountains 39.7314x-115.3231 - Jul 29, 2014, 8:08 PM	L3011820	P	39.7313880	-115.3231200	2014-07-29	20:08:00	obsr111092	S19291721	Traveling	P22	EBIRD	210	1.931		1	1		0	1	0		This observations begin on 29 July and end at 9:45 am on 30 July. The site is ~2 miles E of County Road 3 up a Cyn in the Butte Mountains for which there was the vaguest of tracks to drive. Near my camp the Cyn bottom is grassy with sparse Artemisia and saltbush. Higher up the Cyn floor has more Pinyon and Juniper. I surmise that the area was heavily impacted by miners whenever that was. 100+ years ago?  Rock formations were chipped and rubble remains below. My hike up the canyon ended at 39.72735. -115.30565, which is 1.6 km straight line from my start point (my camp). So I hiked at least 3.2km round trip.  End point elev is between 6919' and 6869'.  Peregrine eyrie on the south cyn wall with, I think, a sub-ad bird tending. I was surprised to not see any Parids here.
